\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_ga35cb54636e53721f2305beb769686bf7}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!computeNECRawDataAndChecksum@{computeNECRawDataAndChecksum}}
\index{computeNECRawDataAndChecksum@{computeNECRawDataAndChecksum}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeNECRawDataAndChecksum()}{computeNECRawDataAndChecksum()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_ga35cb54636e53721f2305beb769686bf7} 
uint32\+\_\+t compute\+NECRaw\+Data\+And\+Checksum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{a\+Address}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{a\+Command}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Convert 16 bit address and 16 bit command to 32 bit NECRaw data If we get a command \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0x100, we send command and then \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}command If we get an address \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0x100, we send 8 bit address and then \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}address !!! Be aware, that this is flexible, but makes it impossible to send e.\+g. 0x0042 as 16 bit value!!! To force send 16 bit address, use\+: \doxylink{group__Decoder_gabef0f59ad36a25a35126172b62c97474}{send\+Onkyo()}.

\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_ga043e7f3939e3832071bd83748f0232bf}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!sendApple@{sendApple}}
\index{sendApple@{sendApple}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendApple()}{sendApple()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_ga043e7f3939e3832071bd83748f0232bf} 
void send\+Apple (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{a\+Device\+Id}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{a\+Command}{, }\item[{int\+\_\+fast8\+\_\+t}]{a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Apple\+: Send NEC with fixed 16 bit Apple address 0x87\+EE. There is NO delay after the last sent repeat! \href{https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apple_Remote}{\texttt{ https\+://en.\+wikipedia.\+org/wiki/\+Apple\+\_\+\+Remote}} \href{https://gist.github.com/darconeous/4437f79a34e3b6441628}{\texttt{ https\+://gist.\+github.\+com/darconeous/4437f79a34e3b6441628}} 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats} & If \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0 then only a special repeat frame without leading and trailing space will be sent by calling NECProtocol\+Constants.\+Special\+Send\+Repeat\+Function(). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_gac85d4b3ebee8ccaff8c32b1ac1ef47a8}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!sendJVCMSB@{sendJVCMSB}}
\index{sendJVCMSB@{sendJVCMSB}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendJVCMSB()}{sendJVCMSB()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_gac85d4b3ebee8ccaff8c32b1ac1ef47a8} 
void send\+JVCMSB (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned long}]{data}{, }\item[{int}]{nbits}{, }\item[{bool}]{repeat}{ = {\ttfamily false}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

With Send \doxylink{group__Decoder_gac85d4b3ebee8ccaff8c32b1ac1ef47a8}{send\+JVCMSB()} you can send your old 32 bit codes. To convert one into the other, you must reverse the byte positions and then reverse all bit positions of each byte. Use bitreverse32\+Bit(). Or write it as one binary string and reverse/mirror it. Example\+: 0x\+CB340102 byte reverse -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 02 01 34 CB bit reverse-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 40 80 2C D3. 0x\+CB340102 is binary 11001011001101000000000100000010. 0x40802\+CD3 is binary 01000000100000000010110011010011. If you read the first binary sequence backwards (right to left), you get the second sequence. 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_ga86fb63d8460828c733054381576affca}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!sendNECMSB@{sendNECMSB}}
\index{sendNECMSB@{sendNECMSB}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendNECMSB()}{sendNECMSB()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_ga86fb63d8460828c733054381576affca} 
void send\+NECMSB (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{data}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{nbits}{, }\item[{bool}]{repeat}{ = {\ttfamily false}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

With Send \doxylink{group__Decoder_ga86fb63d8460828c733054381576affca}{send\+NECMSB()} you can send your old 32 bit codes. To convert one into the other, you must reverse the byte positions and then reverse all bit positions of each byte. Use bitreverse32\+Bit(). Or write it as one binary string and reverse/mirror it. Example\+: 0x\+CB340102 byte reverse -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 02 01 34 CB bit reverse-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 40 80 2C D3. 0x\+CB340102 is binary 11001011001101000000000100000010. 0x40802\+CD3 is binary 01000000100000000010110011010011. If you read the first binary sequence backwards (right to left), you get the second sequence.

\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}

\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_ga48caee41acdca20f481b210353a45e98}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!sendPronto@{sendPronto}}
\index{sendPronto@{sendPronto}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendPronto()}{sendPronto()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_ga48caee41acdca20f481b210353a45e98} 
void send\+Pronto (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{str}{, }\item[{int\+\_\+fast8\+\_\+t}]{a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{IRremoteInt_8h_a5d35fb37031b53f0083f8b88ae3cf2c2}{NO\+\_\+\+REPEATS}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Parse the string given as Pronto Hex, and send it a number of times given as the second argument. Thereby the division of the Pronto Hex into an intro-\/sequence and a repeat sequence is taken into account\+: First the intro sequence is sent, then the repeat sequence is sent times-\/1 times. However, if the intro sequence is empty, the repeat sequence is sent times times. \href{http://www.harctoolbox.org/Glossary.html\#ProntoSemantics}{\texttt{ Reference}}.

Note\+: Using this function is very wasteful for the memory consumption on a small board. Normally it is a much better idea to use a tool like e.\+g. Ir\+Scrutinizer to transform Pronto type signals offline to a more memory efficient format.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em str} & C type string (null terminated) containing a Pronto Hex representation. \\
\hline
{\em a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats} & Number of times to send the signal. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ len\ =\ strlen(str)\ /\ (digitsInProntoNumber\ +\ 1)\ +\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \ \ \ \ uint16\_t\ data[len];}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00421\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}

\end{DoxyCode}
\Hypertarget{group__Decoder_ga8b68c7ff32da204dc5c9dd535d4b0f74}\index{Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}!sendSamsung@{sendSamsung}}
\index{sendSamsung@{sendSamsung}!Decoders and encoders for different protocols@{Decoders and encoders for different protocols}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendSamsung()}{sendSamsung()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__Decoder_ga8b68c7ff32da204dc5c9dd535d4b0f74} 
void send\+Samsung (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{a\+Address}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{a\+Command}{, }\item[{int\+\_\+fast8\+\_\+t}]{a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Here we send Samsung32 If we get a command \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0x100, we send command and then \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}command If we get an address \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0x100, we send 8 bit address and then the same 8 bit address again, this makes it flipper IRDB compatible !!! Be aware, that this is flexible, but makes it impossible to send e.\+g. 0x0042 as 16 bit value!!! To force send 16 bit address, use\+: \doxylink{group__Decoder_ga532399b0d6e76ed7a5477f5455ae8656}{send\+Samsung16\+Bit\+Address\+And\+Command()}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em a\+Number\+Of\+Repeats} & If \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0 then only a special repeat frame will be sent \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
